msg:I bought a room voucher on a certain website very early and chose between two Songpin hotels in Changxing and Wuxi. After reading the reviews, I decisively chose Changxing Songpin Hotel. It was indeed a worthwhile trip. The hotel left a good impression on us and we must give it a big thumbs up üëç. I have stayed in many luxury resort hotels, and this was my first time at Songpin Hotel. After three days and two nights of stay, my eyes lit up.


First of all, the hardware, imitating Song Dynasty style architecture, the overall garden design is grand and beautiful, the pavilions, pavilions and small garden scenes are elegant, profound and interesting. Move and change scenery. The interior decoration design is also in the new Chinese style, with dark furniture and hard furnishings, combined with plain floors and soft furnishings. It is simple, calm and warm. With the central space and floor heating, I can enjoy tea comfortably in the cold wind and rain. Bai, didn't want to move at all. In addition, a Villeroy & Boch integrated toilet is used, and the other bathroom fixtures are all Hansgrohe, which is of good taste. The tea is Wang Chuande's unique Dianhong and Heipu, and the drinking water is Bama Platinum Spring, unlimited. I usually drink tea, and I know a little bit about it. Many dim sum in hotels of the same level mostly use their own tea bags and original tea. It is impossible to say how good the quality and taste are. The food in the hotel is exquisite, and the chef's skills are good, so I had two dinners here. The other configurations in the set are all there, and they are only higher than the upper limit of the same level.


In terms of software, Changxing Songpin‚Äôs operations team is unique. There are 42 rooms, small and sophisticated, and there don‚Äôt seem to be many staff, but the service is real and at your fingertips. In particular, guest service manager Cai contacted me early and added WeChat, asking for our needs and help many times. We were also given an unexpected surprise and were upgraded to a suite. No matter which depar**ent the hotel employees work in, whether in the lobby, guest rooms, security, or restaurants, they always maintain a posture of being ready to provide services when facing guests. Most of the time, the guests do not need to speak, just make eye contact, and the staff will understand. And proactively offer help. A few small details: Ms. Zhang at the front desk and the waiter named Wang held umbrellas for us and took our luggage to the guest room. After checking out, the lady at the front desk sent us to the underground garage, and the room attendant brought us a small bed. The layout of the hotel rooms is circuitous, and those who don‚Äôt know how to ask for help will guide us to our destination. The hotel is also very kid-friendly, with fan painting, paper cutting, calligraphy and embroidery available. The children had a great time playing. It was cold and rainy, so Manager Cai asked the restaurant to deliver a sumptuous breakfast to the guest room. Generally speaking, Changxing Songpin's service is meticulous and considerate from the heart, but also very well-measured, making people happy with beauty and emotion. Butler-style services have become popular in the past two years, but many of them are just formalities and gimmicks. Although there are no butlers in Changxing Songpin, every staff member here can be a butler. They smile, take initiative, step forward, and follow up. Each has its own division of labor, so that guests can The goals of satisfaction are all the same, and your reasonable needs can be met. During the few days we stayed at Changxing Songpin, the hotel left a good impression on us and made us feel at home. I give full marks to such a team in terms of professionalism, discipline, and service. Finally, my evaluation of this hotel is that the hotel itself is an excellent experience. I would like to thank the hotel for its warm reception, attentive and thoughtful service and highly recommend it.
